<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Compression codec. one of following : gzip, bzip2, lzo, lzop, snappy</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
hdfs.fileType</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
SequenceFile</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
File format: currently <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">SequenceFile</span></tt>, <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">DataStream</span></tt> or <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">CompressedStream</span></tt> (1)DataStream
 will not compress output file and please don’t set codeC (2)CompressedStream requires set hdfs.codeC with an available codeC</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
hdfs.maxOpenFiles</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
5000</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Allow only this number of open files. If this number is exceeded, the oldest file is closed.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
hdfs.minBlockReplicas</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Specify minimum number of replicas per HDFS block. If not specified, it comes from the default Hadoop config in the classpath.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
hdfs.writeFormat</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Format for sequence file records. One of “Text” or “Writable” (the default).</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
hdfs.callTimeout</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
10000</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Number of milliseconds allowed for HDFS operations, such as open, write, flush, close. This number should be increased if many HDFS timeout operations are occurring.</td>

<tr class="row-even">

hdfs.threadsPoolSize</td>

10</td>

Should the timestamp be rounded down (if true, affects all time based escape sequences except %t)</td>

<tr class="row-even">

hdfs.roundValue</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
1</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Rounded down to the highest multiple of this (in the unit configured using <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">hdfs.roundUnit</span></tt>),
 less than current time.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">

hdfs.roundUnit</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
second</td>

The unit of the round down value - <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">second</span></tt>, <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">minute</span></tt> or <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">hour</span></tt>.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">

hdfs.timeZone</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Local Time</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Name of the timezone that should be used for resolving the directory path, e.g. America/Los_Angeles.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
hdfs.useLocalTimeStamp</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
false</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Use the local time (instead of the timestamp from the event header) while replacing the escape sequences.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
serializer</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">TEXT</span></tt></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Other possible options include <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">avro_event</span></tt> or the fully-qualified
 class name of an implementation of the<tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">EventSerializer.Builder</span></tt> interface.</td>
</tr>

serializer.*</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
 </td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
 </td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">k1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.type</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">hdfs</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.channel</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.hdfs.path</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/flume/events/%y-%m-%d/%H%M/%S</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.hdfs.filePrefix</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">events-</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.hdfs.round</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">true</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.hdfs.roundValue</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">10</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.hdfs.roundUnit</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">minute</span>
</pre>
</div>
</div>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The above configuration will round down the timestamp to the last 10th minute. For example, an event with timestamp 11:54:34 AM, June 12, 2012 will cause the hdfs path to become <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">/flume/events/2012-06-12/1150/00</span></tt>.</p>
</div>
<div id="logger-sink" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t58"></a>Logger Sink</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Logs event at INFO level. Typically useful for testing/debugging purpose. Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">

<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>channel</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
 </td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, needs to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">logger</span></tt></td>

<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">

<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>

<div id="avro-sink" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t59"></a>Avro Sink</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This sink forms one half of Flume’s tiered collection support. Flume events sent to this sink are turned into Avro events and sent to the configured hostname / port pair. The events are taken from the configured
 Channel in batches of the configured batch size. Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="7%"><col width="2%"><col width="91%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>

<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>channel</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
 </td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, needs to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">avro</span></tt>.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>hostname</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The hostname or IP address to bind to.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>port</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The port # to listen on.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
batch-size</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
100</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
number of event to batch together for send.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
connect-timeout</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
20000</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Amount of time (ms) to allow for the first (handshake) request.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
request-timeout</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
20000</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Amount of time (ms) to allow for requests after the first.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
reset-connection-interval</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
none</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Amount of time (s) before the connection to the next hop is reset. This will force the Avro Sink to reconnect to the next hop. This will allow the sink to connect to hosts behind a hardware load-balancer when news hosts are added without having to restart the
 agent.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
compression-type</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
none</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
This can be “none” or “deflate”. The compression-type must match the compression-type of matching AvroSource</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
compression-level</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
6</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The level of compression to compress event. 0 = no compression and 1-9 is compression. The higher the number the more compression</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
ssl</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
false</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Set to true to enable SSL for this AvroSink. When configuring SSL, you can optionally set a “truststore”, “truststore-password”, “truststore-type”, and specify whether to “trust-all-certs”.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
trust-all-certs</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
false</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
If this is set to true, SSL server certificates for remote servers (Avro Sources) will not be checked. This should NOT be used in production because it makes it easier for an attacker to execute a man-in-the-middle attack and “listen in” on the encrypted connection.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
truststore</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The path to a custom Java truststore file. Flume uses the certificate authority information in this file to determine whether the remote Avro Source’s SSL authentication credentials should be trusted. If not specified, the default Java JSSE certificate authority
 files (typically “jssecacerts” or “cacerts” in the Oracle JRE) will be used.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
truststore-password</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The password for the specified truststore.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
truststore-type</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
JKS</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The type of the Java truststore. This can be “JKS” or other supported Java truststore type.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.channel</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>

<div id="thrift-sink" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t60"></a>Thrift Sink</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This sink forms one half of Flume’s tiered collection support. Flume events sent to this sink are turned into Thrift events and sent to the configured hostname / port pair. The events are taken from the configured
 Channel in batches of the configured batch size. Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>

<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">

number of event to batch together for send.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
connect-timeout</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
20000</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Amount of time (ms) to allow for the first (handshake) request.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
request-timeout</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
20000</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Amount of time (ms) to allow for requests after the first.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
connection-reset-interval</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
none</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Amount of time (s) before the connection to the next hop is reset. This will force the Thrift Sink to reconnect to the next hop. This will allow the sink to connect to hosts behind a hardware load-balancer when news hosts are added without having to restart
 the agent.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">k1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.type</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">thrift</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.channel</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.hostname</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">10.10.10.10</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.port</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">4545</span>

<div id="file-roll-sink" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">

Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">

<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">

 </td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">

<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, needs to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">file_roll</span></tt>.</td>

<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>sink.directory</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The directory where files will be stored</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
sink.rollInterval</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
30</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Roll the file every 30 seconds. Specifying 0 will disable rolling and cause all events to be written to a single file.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
sink.serializer</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
TEXT</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Other possible options include <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">avro_event</span></tt> or the FQCN of an implementation
 of EventSerializer.Builder interface.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
batchSize</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
100</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
 </td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<div id="hbasesinks" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t64"></a>HBaseSinks</h4>
<div id="hbasesink" class="section">
<h5 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:18px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t65"></a>HBaseSink</h5>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This sink writes data to HBase. The Hbase configuration is picked up from the first hbase-site.xml encountered in the classpath. A class implementing HbaseEventSerializer which is specified by the configuration
 is used to convert the events into HBase puts and/or increments. These puts and increments are then written to HBase. This sink provides the same consistency guarantees as HBase, which is currently row-wise atomicity. In the event of Hbase failing to write
 certain events, the sink will replay all events in that transaction.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The HBaseSink supports writing data to secure HBase. To write to secure HBase, the user the agent is running as must have write permissions to the table the sink is configured to write to. The principal and keytab
 to use to authenticate against the KDC can be specified in the configuration. The hbase-site.xml in the Flume agent’s classpath must have authentication set to <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">kerberos</span></tt> (For
 details on how to do this, please refer to HBase documentation).</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">For convenience, two serializers are provided with Flume. The SimpleHbaseEventSerializer (org.apache.flume.sink.hbase.SimpleHbaseEventSerializer) writes the event body as-is to HBase, and optionally increments
 a column in Hbase. This is primarily an example implementation. The RegexHbaseEventSerializer (org.apache.flume.sink.hbase.RegexHbaseEventSerializer) breaks the event body based on the given regex and writes each part into different columns.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The type is the FQCN: org.apache.flume.sink.hbase.HBaseSink.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">

<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">

<div id="asynchbasesink" class="section">
<h5 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:18px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t66"></a>AsyncHBaseSink</h5>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This sink writes data to HBase using an asynchronous model. A class implementing AsyncHbaseEventSerializer which is specified by the configuration is used to convert the events into HBase puts and/or increments.
 These puts and increments are then written to HBase. This sink provides the same consistency guarantees as HBase, which is currently row-wise atomicity. In the event of Hbase failing to write certain events, the sink will replay all events in that transaction.
 The type is the FQCN: org.apache.flume.sink.hbase.AsyncHBaseSink. Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">

<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">

–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, needs to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">asynchbase</span></tt></td>

<tr class="row-even">

<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Note that this sink takes the Zookeeper Quorum and parent znode information in the configuration. Zookeeper Quorum and parent node configuration may be specified in the flume configuration file. Alternatively,
 these configuration values are taken from the first hbase-site.xml file in the classpath.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">If these are not provided in the configuration, then the sink will read this information from the first hbase-site.xml file in the classpath.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1:</p>

<div id="morphlinesolrsink" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t67"></a>MorphlineSolrSink</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This sink extracts data from Flume events, transforms it, and loads it in near-real-time into Apache Solr servers, which in turn serve queries to end users or search applications.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This sink is well suited for use cases that stream raw data into HDFS (via the HdfsSink) and simultaneously extract, transform and load the same data into Solr (via MorphlineSolrSink). In particular, this sink
 can process arbitrary heterogeneous raw data from disparate data sources and turn it into a data model that is useful to Search applications.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The ETL functionality is customizable using a <a target="_blank" class="reference external" href="http://cloudera.github.io/cdk/docs/0.4.0/cdk-morphlines/index.html" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(53,95,124); text-decoration:none">morphline
 configuration file</a> that defines a chain of transformation commands that pipe event records from one command to another.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Morphlines can be seen as an evolution of Unix pipelines where the data model is generalized to work with streams of generic records, including arbitrary binary payloads. A morphline command is a bit like a Flume
 Interceptor. Morphlines can be embedded into Hadoop components such as Flume.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Commands to parse and transform a set of standard data formats such as log files, Avro, CSV, Text, HTML, XML, PDF, Word, Excel, etc. are provided out of the box, and additional custom commands and parsers for
 additional data formats can be added as morphline plugins. Any kind of data format can be indexed and any Solr documents for any kind of Solr schema can be generated, and any custom ETL logic can be registered and executed.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Morphlines manipulate continuous streams of records. The data model can be described as follows: A record is a set of named fields where each field has an ordered list of one or more values. A value can be any
 Java Object. That is, a record is essentially a hash table where each hash table entry contains a String key and a list of Java Objects as values. (The implementation uses Guava’s <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">ArrayListMultimap</span></tt>,
 which is a <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">ListMultimap</span></tt>). Note that a field can have multiple values
 and any two records need not use common field names.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This sink fills the body of the Flume event into the <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">_attachment_body</span></tt> field
 of the morphline record, as well as copies the headers of the Flume event into record fields of the same name. The commands can then act on this data.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Routing to a SolrCloud cluster is supported to improve scalability. Indexing load can be spread across a large number of MorphlineSolrSinks for improved scalability. Indexing load can be replicated across multiple
 MorphlineSolrSinks for high availability, for example using Flume features such as Load balancing Sink Processor. MorphlineInterceptor can also help to implement dynamic routing to multiple Solr collections (e.g. for multi-tenancy).</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The morphline and solr jars required for your environment must be placed in the lib directory of the Apache Flume installation.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The type is the FQCN: org.apache.flume.sink.solr.morphline.MorphlineSolrSink</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="8%"><col width="30%"><col width="62%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">

Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>

<div id="elasticsearchsink" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t68"></a>ElasticSearchSink</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This sink writes data to an elasticsearch cluster. By default, events will be written so that the <a target="_blank" class="reference external" href="http://kibana.org/" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(53,95,124); text-decoration:none">Kibana</a> graphical
 interface can display them - just as if <a target="_blank" class="reference external" href="https://logstash.net/" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(53,95,124); text-decoration:none">logstash</a> wrote them.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The elasticsearch and lucene-core jars required for your environment must be placed in the lib directory of the Apache Flume installation. Elasticsearch requires that the major version of the client JAR match
 that of the server and that both are running the same minor version of the JVM. SerializationExceptions will appear if this is incorrect. To select the required version first determine the version of elasticsearch and the JVM version the target cluster is
 running. Then select an elasticsearch client library which matches the major version. A 0.19.x client can talk to a 0.19.x cluster; 0.20.x can talk to 0.20.x and 0.90.x can talk to 0.90.x. Once the elasticsearch version has been determined then read the pom.xml
 file to determine the correct lucene-core JAR version to use. The Flume agent which is running the ElasticSearchSink should also match the JVM the target cluster is running down to the minor version.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Events will be written to a new index every day. The name will be &lt;indexName&gt;-yyyy-MM-dd where &lt;indexName&gt; is the indexName parameter. The sink will start writing to a new index at midnight UTC.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Events are serialized for elasticsearch by the ElasticSearchLogStashEventSerializer by default. This behaviour can be overridden with the serializer parameter. This parameter accepts implementations of org.apache.flume.sink.elasticsearch.ElasticSearchEventSerializer
 or org.apache.flume.sink.elasticsearch.ElasticSearchIndexRequestBuilderFactory. Implementing ElasticSearchEventSerializer is deprecated in favour of the more powerful ElasticSearchIndexRequestBuilderFactory.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The type is the FQCN: org.apache.flume.sink.elasticsearch.ElasticSearchSink</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">

<div id="custom-sink" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t69"></a>Custom Sink</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">A custom sink is your own implementation of the Sink interface. A custom sink’s class and its dependencies must be included in the agent’s classpath when starting the Flume agent. The type of the custom sink is
 its FQCN. Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">

<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">

Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>

<strong>channel</strong></td>

<div id="flume-channels" class="section">
<h3 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:22px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t70"></a>Flume Channels</h3>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Channels are the repositories where the events are staged on a agent. Source adds the events and Sink removes it.</p>
<div id="memory-channel" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t71"></a>Memory Channel</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The events are stored in an in-memory queue with configurable max size. It’s ideal for flows that need higher throughput and are prepared to lose the staged data in the event of a agent failures. Required properties
 are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="22%"><col width="13%"><col width="65%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">

<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, needs to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">memory</span></tt></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
capacity</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
100</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The maximum number of events stored in the channel</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
transactionCapacity</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
100</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The maximum number of events the channel will take from a source or give to a sink per transaction</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
keep-alive</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
3</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Timeout in seconds for adding or removing an event</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
byteCapacityBufferPercentage</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
20</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Defines the percent of buffer between byteCapacity and the estimated total size of all events in the channel, to account for data in headers. See below.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
byteCapacity</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
see description</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Maximum total <strong>bytes</strong> of memory allowed as a sum of all events in this channel. The implementation only counts the Event <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">body</span></tt>,
 which is the reason for providing the<tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">byteCapacityBufferPercentage</span></tt> configuration
 parameter as well. Defaults to a computed value equal to 80% of the maximum memory available to the JVM (i.e. 80% of the -Xmx value passed on the command line). Note that if you have multiple memory channels on a single JVM, and they happen to hold the same
 physical events (i.e. if you are using a replicating channel selector from a single source) then those event sizes may be double-counted for channel byteCapacity purposes. Setting this value to <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">0</span></tt> will
 cause this value to fall back to a hard internal limit of about 200 GB.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.type</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">memory</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.capacity</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">10000</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.transactionCapacity</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">10000</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.byteCapacityBufferPercentage</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">20</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.byteCapacity</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">800000</span>
</pre>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="jdbc-channel" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t72"></a>JDBC Channel</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The events are stored in a persistent storage that’s backed by a database. The JDBC channel currently supports embedded Derby. This is a durable channel that’s ideal for flows where recoverability is important.
 Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">

<div id="file-channel" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t73"></a>File Channel</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="21%"><col width="14%"><col width="65%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
 </th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, needs to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">file</span></tt>.</td>
</tr>

<div class="admonition note" style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; border-left:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:7px; background-color:rgb(238,238,238); margin-top:10px; padding-left:7px; padding-right:7px; margin-bottom:10px; border-top:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; border-right:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-top:7px">
<p class="first admonition-title" style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px; margin-top:0px; display:inline; margin-bottom:5px; font-weight:bold; margin-right:10px">
Note</p>
 
<p class="last" style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px; display:inline; margin-bottom:5px">
By default the File Channel uses paths for checkpoint and data directories that are within the user home as specified above. As a result if you have more than one File Channel instances active within the agent, only one will be able to lock the directories
 and cause the other channel initialization to fail. It is therefore necessary that you provide explicit paths to all the configured channels, preferably on different disks. Furthermore, as file channel will sync to disk after every commit, coupling it with
 a sink/source that batches events together may be necessary to provide good performance where multiple disks are not available for checkpoint and data directories.</p>
</div>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.type</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">file</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.checkpointDir</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/mnt/flume/checkpoint</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.dataDirs</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/mnt/flume/data</span>
</pre>
</div>
</div>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px"><strong>Encryption</strong></p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Below is a few sample configurations:</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Generating a key with a password seperate from the key store password:</p>
<div class="highlight-bash">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px">keytool -genseckey -alias key-0 -keypass keyPassword -keyalg AES <span class="se" style="color:#bb8844">\</span>
  -keysize 128 -validity 9000 -keystore test.keystore <span class="se" style="color:#bb8844">\</span>
  -storetype jceks -storepass keyStorePassword
</pre>
</div>
</div>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Generating a key with the password the same as the key store password:</p>
<div class="highlight-bash">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px">keytool -genseckey -alias key-1 -keyalg AES -keysize 128 -validity 9000 <span class="se" style="color:#bb8844">\</span>
  -keystore src/test/resources/test.keystore -storetype jceks <span class="se" style="color:#bb8844">\</span>
  -storepass keyStorePassword
</pre>
</div>
</div>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.activeKey</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">key-0</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.cipherProvider</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">AESCTRNOPADDING</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">key-provider-0</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">JCEKSFILE</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider.keyStoreFile</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/path/to/my.keystore</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider.keyStorePasswordFile</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/path/to/my.keystore.password</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider.keys</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">key-0</span>
</pre>
</div>
</div>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Let’s say you have aged key-0 out and new files should be encrypted with key-1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.activeKey</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">key-1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.cipherProvider</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">AESCTRNOPADDING</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">JCEKSFILE</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider.keyStoreFile</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/path/to/my.keystore</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider.keyStorePasswordFile</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/path/to/my.keystore.password</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider.keys</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">key-0 key-1</span>
</pre>
</div>
</div>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The same scenerio as above, however key-0 has its own password:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.activeKey</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">key-1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.cipherProvider</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">AESCTRNOPADDING</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">JCEKSFILE</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider.keyStoreFile</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/path/to/my.keystore</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider.keyStorePasswordFile</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/path/to/my.keystore.password</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider.keys</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">key-0 key-1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.encryption.keyProvider.keys.key-0.passwordFile</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/path/to/key-0.password</span>
</pre>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="pseudo-transaction-channel" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t74"></a>Pseudo Transaction Channel</h4>
<div class="admonition warning" style="border-bottom:rgb(255,102,102) 1px solid; border-left:rgb(255,102,102) 1px solid; padding-bottom:7px; background-color:rgb(255,228,228); margin-top:10px; padding-left:7px; padding-right:7px; margin-bottom:10px; border-top:rgb(255,102,102) 1px solid; border-right:rgb(255,102,102) 1px solid; padding-top:7px">

Warning</p>
 
<p class="last" style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px; display:inline; margin-bottom:5px">
The Pseudo Transaction Channel is only for unit testing purposes and is NOT meant for production use.</p>
