<div id="custom-channel" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t75"></a>Custom Channel</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">A custom channel is your own implementation of the Channel interface. A custom channel’s class and its dependencies must be included in the agent’s classpath when starting the Flume agent. The type of the custom
 channel is its FQCN. Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="15%"><col width="8%"><col width="76%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, needs to be a FQCN</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels.c1.type</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">org.example.MyChannel</span>
</pre>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="flume-channel-selectors" class="section">
<h3 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:22px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t76"></a>Flume Channel Selectors</h3>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">If the type is not specified, then defaults to “replicating”.</p>
<div id="replicating-channel-selector-default" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t77"></a>Replicating Channel Selector (default)</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="22%"><col width="14%"><col width="64%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
selector.type</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
replicating</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, needs to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">replicating</span></tt></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
selector.optional</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Set of channels to be marked as <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">optional</span></tt></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1 and it’s source called r1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sources</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">r1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1 c2 c3</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.source.r1.selector.type</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">replicating</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.source.r1.channels</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1 c2 c3</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.source.r1.selector.optional</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c3</span>
</pre>
</div>
</div>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">In the above configuration, c3 is an optional channel. Failure to write to c3 is simply ignored. Since c1 and c2 are not marked optional, failure to write to those channels will cause the transaction to fail.</p>
</div>

<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1 and it’s source called r1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">

<div id="custom-channel-selector" class="section">

<a target="_blank" name="t79"></a>Custom Channel Selector</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">A custom channel selector is your own implementation of the ChannelSelector interface. A custom channel selector’s class and its dependencies must be included in the agent’s classpath when starting the Flume agent.
 The type of the custom channel selector is its FQCN.</p>

<div id="flume-sink-processors" class="section">
<h3 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:22px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t80"></a>Flume Sink Processors</h3>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Sink groups allow users to group multiple sinks into one entity. Sink processors can be used to provide load balancing capabilities over all sinks inside the group or to achieve fail over from one sink to another
 in case of temporal failure.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">

Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>

The component type name, needs to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">default</span></tt>, <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">failover</span></tt> or <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">load_balance</span></tt></td>

<div id="default-sink-processor" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t81"></a>Default Sink Processor</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Default sink processor accepts only a single sink. User is not forced to create processor (sink group) for single sinks. Instead user can follow the source - channel - sink pattern that was explained above in
 this user guide.</p>
</div>
<div id="failover-sink-processor" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t82"></a>Failover Sink Processor</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Failover Sink Processor maintains a prioritized list of sinks, guaranteeing that so long as one is available events will be processed (delivered).</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The failover mechanism works by relegating failed sinks to a pool where they are assigned a cool down period, increasing with sequential failures before they are retried. Once a sink successfully sends an event,
 it is restored to the live pool.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">To configure, set a sink groups processor to <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">failover</span></tt> and
 set priorities for all individual sinks. All specified priorities must be unique. Furthermore, upper limit to failover time can be set (in milliseconds) using <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">maxpenalty</span></tt> property.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="26%"><col width="9%"><col width="66%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">

<strong>sinks</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Space-separated list of sinks that are participating in the group</td>

<tr class="row-odd">

<strong>processor.type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">default</span></tt></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, needs to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">failover</span></tt></td>

<strong>processor.priority.&lt;sinkName&gt;</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">

30000</td>

(in millis)</td>
</tr>

<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinkgroups.g1.sinks</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">k1 k2</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinkgroups.g1.processor.type</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">failover</span>

<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinkgroups.g1.processor.priority.k2</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">10</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinkgroups.g1.processor.maxpenalty</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">10000</span>

<div id="load-balancing-sink-processor" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t83"></a>Load balancing Sink Processor</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Load balancing sink processor provides the ability to load-balance flow over multiple sinks. It maintains an indexed list of active sinks on which the load must be distributed. Implementation supports distributing
 load using either via <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">round_robin</span></tt> or <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">random</span></tt> selection
 mechanisms. The choice of selection mechanism defaults to <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">round_robin</span></tt> type,
 but can be overridden via configuration. Custom selection mechanisms are supported via custom classes that inherits from <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">AbstractSinkSelector</span></tt>.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">When invoked, this selector picks the next sink using its configured selection mechanism and invokes it. For <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">round_robin</span></tt> and <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">random</span></tt> In
 case the selected sink fails to deliver the event, the processor picks the next available sink via its configured selection mechanism. This implementation does not blacklist the failing sink and instead continues to optimistically attempt every available sink.
 If all sinks invocations result in failure, the selector propagates the failure to the sink runner.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">If <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">backoff</span></tt> is enabled,
 the sink processor will blacklist sinks that fail, removing them for selection for a given timeout. When the timeout ends, if the sink is still unresponsive timeout is increased exponentially to avoid potentially getting stuck in long waits on unresponsive
 sinks. With this disabled, in round-robin all the failed sinks load will be passed to the next sink in line and thus not evenly balanced</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="25%"><col width="13%"><col width="63%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>processor.sinks</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Space-separated list of sinks that are participating in the group</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>processor.type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">default</span></tt></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, needs to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">load_balance</span></tt></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
processor.backoff</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
false</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Should failed sinks be backed off exponentially.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">

processor.selector</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">round_robin</span></tt></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Selection mechanism. Must be either <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">round_robin</span></tt>, <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">random</span></tt> or
 FQCN of custom class that inherits from <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">AbstractSinkSelector</span></tt></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
processor.selector.maxTimeOut</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
30000</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Used by backoff selectors to limit exponential backoff (in milliseconds)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinkgroups</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">g1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinkgroups.g1.sinks</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">k1 k2</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinkgroups.g1.processor.type</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">load_balance</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinkgroups.g1.processor.backoff</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">true</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinkgroups.g1.processor.selector</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">random</span>
</pre>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="custom-sink-processor" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t84"></a>Custom Sink Processor</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Custom sink processors are not supported at the moment.</p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="event-serializers" class="section">
<h3 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:22px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t85"></a>Event Serializers</h3>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">file_roll</span></tt> sink
 and the <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">hdfs</span></tt> sink both support the <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">EventSerializer</span></tt> interface.
 Details of the EventSerializers that ship with Flume are provided below.</p>
<div id="body-text-serializer" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t86"></a>Body Text Serializer</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Alias: <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">text</span></tt>. This
 interceptor writes the body of the event to an output stream without any transformation or modification. The event headers are ignored. Configuration options are as follows:</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="22%"><col width="14%"><col width="65%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
appendNewline</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
true</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Whether a newline will be appended to each event at write time. The default of true assumes that events do not contain newlines, for legacy reasons.</td>
</tr>

</table>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">k1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.type</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">file_roll</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.channel</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.sink.directory</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/var/log/flume</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.sink.serializer</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">text</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.sink.serializer.appendNewline</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">false</span>

<div id="avro-event-serializer" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t87"></a>Avro Event Serializer</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Alias: <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">avro_event</span></tt>.
 This interceptor serializes Flume events into an Avro container file. The schema used is the same schema used for Flume events in the Avro RPC mechanism. This serializers inherits from the <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">AbstractAvroEventSerializer</span></tt> class.
 Configuration options are as follows:</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="22%"><col width="14%"><col width="64%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
syncIntervalBytes</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
2048000</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Avro sync interval, in approximate bytes.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">

compressionCodec</td>

null</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Avro compression codec. For supported codecs, see Avro’s CodecFactory docs.</td>
</tr>

</table>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">

<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.channel</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.hdfs.path</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">/flume/events/%y-%m-%d/%H%M/%S</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.serializer</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">avro_event</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.serializer.compressionCodec</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">snappy</span>

<div id="flume-interceptors" class="section">
<h3 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:22px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t88"></a>Flume Interceptors</h3>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Flume has the capability to modify/drop events in-flight. This is done with the help of interceptors. Interceptors are classes that implement<tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">org.apache.flume.interceptor.Interceptor</span></tt> interface.
 An interceptor can modify or even drop events based on any criteria chosen by the developer of the interceptor. Flume supports chaining of interceptors. This is made possible through by specifying the list of interceptor builder class names in the configuration.
 Interceptors are specified as a whitespace separated list in the source configuration. The order in which the interceptors are specified is the order in which they are invoked. The list of events returned by one interceptor is passed to the next interceptor
 in the chain. Interceptors can modify or drop events. If an interceptor needs to drop events, it just does not return that event in the list that it returns. If it is to drop all events, then it simply returns an empty list. Interceptors are named components,
 here is an example of how they are created through configuration:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">
<pre style="border-bottom:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-bottom:5px; line-height:15px; overflow-x:auto; overflow-y:hidden; border-right-style:none; background-color:rgb(238,255,204); padding-left:5px; padding-right:5px; color:rgb(51,51,51); border-left-style:none; border-top:rgb(170,204,153) 1px solid; padding-top:5px"><span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sources</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">r1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">k1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.channels</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sources.r1.interceptors</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">i1 i2</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sources.r1.interceptors.i1.type</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">org.apache.flume.interceptor.HostInterceptor$Builder</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sources.r1.interceptors.i1.preserveExisting</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">false</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sources.r1.interceptors.i1.hostHeader</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">hostname</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sources.r1.interceptors.i2.type</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">org.apache.flume.interceptor.TimestampInterceptor$Builder</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.filePrefix</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">FlumeData.%{CollectorHost}.%Y-%m-%d</span>
<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sinks.k1.channel</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">c1</span>
</pre>
</div>
</div>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Note that the interceptor builders are passed to the type config parameter. The interceptors are themselves configurable and can be passed configuration values just like they are passed to any other configurable
 component. In the above example, events are passed to the HostInterceptor first and the events returned by the HostInterceptor are then passed along to the TimestampInterceptor. You can specify either the fully qualified class name (FQCN) or the alias <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">timestamp</span></tt>.
 If you have multiple collectors writing to the same HDFS path, then you could also use the HostInterceptor.</p>
<div id="timestamp-interceptor" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t89"></a>Timestamp Interceptor</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This interceptor inserts into the event headers, the time in millis at which it processes the event. This interceptor inserts a header with key<tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">timestamp</span></tt> whose
 value is the relevant timestamp. This interceptor can preserve an existing timestamp if it is already present in the configuration.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="17%"><col width="7%"><col width="76%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, has to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">timestamp</span></tt> or the FQCN</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">

preserveExisting</td>

false</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
If the timestamp already exists, should it be preserved - true or false</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Example for agent named a1:</p>
<div class="highlight-properties">
<div class="highlight">

<div id="host-interceptor" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t90"></a>Host Interceptor</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This interceptor inserts the hostname or IP address of the host that this agent is running on. It inserts a header with key <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">host</span></tt> or
 a configured key whose value is the hostname or IP address of the host, based on configuration.</p>

Default</th>

useIP</td>

<div id="static-interceptor" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t91"></a>Static Interceptor</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Static interceptor allows user to append a static header with static value to all events.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">The current implementation does not allow specifying multiple headers at one time. Instead user might chain multiple static interceptors each defining one static header.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="16%"><col width="7%"><col width="77%"></colgroup>

Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>

<tr class="row-even">

<strong>type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name, has to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">static</span></tt></td>

If configured header already exists, should it be preserved - true or false</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
key</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
key</td>

<span class="na" style="color:#08080">a1.sources.r1.interceptors.i1.value</span> <span class="o" style="font-weight:bold">=</span> <span class="s" style="color:#bb8844">NEW_YORK</span>

<div id="uuid-interceptor" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t92"></a>UUID Interceptor</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This interceptor sets a universally unique identifier on all events that are intercepted. An example UUID is <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">b5755073-77a9-43c1-8fad-b7a586fc1b97</span></tt>,
 which represents a 128-bit value.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Consider using UUIDInterceptor to automatically assign a UUID to an event if no application level unique key for the event is available. It can be important to assign UUIDs to events as soon as they enter the
 Flume network; that is, in the first Flume Source of the flow. This enables subsequent deduplication of events in the face of replication and redelivery in a Flume network that is designed for high availability and high performance. If an application level
 key is available, this is preferable over an auto-generated UUID because it enables subsequent updates and deletes of event in data stores using said well known application level key.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="13%"><col width="6%"><col width="81%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name has to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">org.apache.flume.sink.solr.morphline.UUIDInterceptor$Builder</span></tt></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
headerName</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
id</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The name of the Flume header to modify</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
preserveExisting</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
true</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
If the UUID header already exists, should it be preserved - true or false</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
prefix</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
“”</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The prefix string constant to prepend to each generated UUID</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
</div>
<div id="morphline-interceptor" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t93"></a>Morphline Interceptor</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This interceptor filters the events through a <a target="_blank" class="reference external" href="http://cloudera.github.io/cdk/docs/0.4.0/cdk-morphlines/index.html" rel="nofollow" style="color:rgb(53,95,124); text-decoration:none">morphline
 configuration file</a> that defines a chain of transformation commands that pipe records from one command to another. For example the morphline can ignore certain events or alter or insert certain event headers via regular expression based pattern matching,
 or it can auto-detect and set a MIME type via Apache Tika on events that are intercepted. For example, this kind of packet sniffing can be used for content based dynamic routing in a Flume topology. MorphlineInterceptor can also help to implement dynamic routing
 to multiple Apache Solr collections (e.g. for multi-tenancy).</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Currently, there is a restriction in that the morphline of an interceptor must not generate more than one output record for each input event. This interceptor is not intended for heavy duty ETL processing - if
 you need this consider moving ETL processing from the Flume Source to a Flume Sink, e.g. to a MorphlineSolrSink.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">Required properties are in <strong>bold</strong>.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="10%"><col width="4%"><col width="85%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name has to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">org.apache.flume.sink.solr.morphline.MorphlineInterceptor$Builder</span></tt></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-odd">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
<strong>morphlineFile</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The relative or absolute path on the local file system to the morphline configuration file. Example: <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">/etc/flume-ng/conf/morphline.conf</span></tt></td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
morphlineId</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
null</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">

</tr>
</tbody>

<div id="regex-filtering-interceptor" class="section">
<h4 style="border-bottom:rgb(204,204,204) 1px solid; padding-bottom:3px; background-color:rgb(242,242,242); margin:20px -20px 10px; padding-left:10px; padding-right:0px; color:rgb(0,0,139); font-size:19px; font-weight:normal; padding-top:3px">
<a target="_blank" name="t94"></a>Regex Filtering Interceptor</h4>
<p style="text-align:justify; line-height:20px">This interceptor filters events selectively by interpreting the event body as text and matching the text against a configured regular expression. The supplied regular expression can be used to include events or
 exclude events.</p>
<table class="docutils" border="1" style="border-bottom:0px; border-left:0px; border-collapse:collapse; border-top:0px; border-right:0px">
<colgroup><col width="17%"><col width="7%"><col width="76%"></colgroup>
<thead valign="bottom">
<tr class="row-odd">
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Property Name</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Default</th>
<th class="head" style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; background-color:rgb(238,221,238); padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody valign="top">
<tr class="row-even">

<strong>type</strong></td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
–</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
The component type name has to be <tt class="docutils literal" style="padding-bottom:0px; background-color:rgb(236,240,243); padding-left:1px; padding-right:1px; font-size:0.95em; padding-top:0px"><span class="pre">regex_filter</span></tt></td>

regex</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
”.*”</td>

Regular expression for matching against events</td>
</tr>
<tr class="row-even">

excludeEvents</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
false</td>
<td style="border-bottom:rgb(170,170,170) 1px solid; padding-bottom:1px; border-right-width:0px; padding-left:5px; padding-right:8px; border-top-width:0px; border-left-width:0px; padding-top:1px">
If true, regex determines events to exclude, otherwise regex determines events to include.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
